<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">up</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*upp</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition_4">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>on, upon
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:melk.html>melk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:staat.html>staat</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tafel.html>tafel</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The milk <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>on</b> the table.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> ... <a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a></span><span class="ib-comma">,</span> with a cardinal number</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:bar.html>bar</a>, except <span class="use-with-mention">Used to form ordinal numbers in relation to a superlative quality. The number that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> 1 lower than in the English translation.</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:naast.html>Naast</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:toonladder.html>toonladder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kenmerkend.html>kenmerkend</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gegeven.html>gegeven</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ook.html>ook</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bepaalde.html>bepaalde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:tonen.html>tonen</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:speciale.html>speciale</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rol.html>rol</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:zoals.html>zoals</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> vadi <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> samvadi, <a href = vnd.unilang:respectievelijk.html>respectievelijk</a>: <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:belangrijkste.html>belangrijkste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:belangrijkste.html>belangrijkste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:toon.html>toon</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Next to [the fact] that the musical scale <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a characteristic datum, there are also certain tones that have a special role, such as the vadi and the samvadi: respectively the most important and <b>second</b> most important tones.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl">Brazilië <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> 8,5 <a href = vnd.unilang:miljoen.html>miljoen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vierkant.html>vierkante</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kilometer.html>kilometer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:grootste.html>grootste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Zuid-Amerika <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vier.html>vier</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>na</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:grootste.html>grootste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ter.html>ter</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wereld.html>wereld</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">With its 8.5 million square <a href = vnd.unilang:kilometers.html>kilometers</a>, Brazil <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the largest country in South America and the <b>fifth</b> largest in the world.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***opal.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:opal.html>opal</a> (17612)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>In Florio’s <i>A World of <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>Words</a></i> 1598 as <i>opale</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">opale</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">opalus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Greek">Byzantine Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ὀπάλλιος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">opállios</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">उपल</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">upala</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">gem, stone</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">उपरि</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">upári</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">the upper millstone</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:opal.html>opal</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">opals</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mineralogy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A mineral consisting, like quartz, of silica, but inferior to quartz in hardness and specific gravity, of the chemical formula SiO<sub>2</sub><b>·</b>NH<sub>2</sub><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>O</a>.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2012</b> March 1,  Lee A. Groat,  “Gemstones”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/American_Scientist" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:American Scientist">American Scientist</a></cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.americanscientist.org/issues/feature/2012/2/gemstones">[1]</a></sup>, volume 100, number 2, page 128:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Although there are dozens of different <a href = vnd.unilang:types.html>types</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:gems.html>gems</a>, among the <a href = vnd.unilang:best.html>best</a> known and most important are [ | ] | . (Common gem materials not addressed in this article include <a href = vnd.unilang:amber.html>amber</a>, amethyst, chalcedony, garnet, lazurite, malachite, <b>opals</b>, peridot, rhodonite, spinel, tourmaline, <a href = vnd.unilang:turquoise.html>turquoise</a> and zircon.)</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">biology<span class="ib-comma">,</span> genetics<span class="ib-comma">,</span> biochemistry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A colloquial name used in molecular biology referring to a particular <a href = vnd.unilang:stop.html>stop</a> codon sequence, "UGA."</li>
<li>Any of various lycaenid butterflies of the genus <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Nesolycaena" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Nesolycaena"><i>Nesolycaena</i></a></span>.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="NavFrame">
<div class="NavHead" style="text-align: left;">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></div>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:opdracht.html>opdracht</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">swelling, transfer</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:opdrachtgever.html>opdrachtgever</a> (18566)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:opdracht.html>opdracht</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gever.html>gever</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:opdrachtgever.html>opdrachtgever</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:opdrachtgevers.html>opdrachtgevers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:opdrachtgever.html>opdrachtgevertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">opdrachtgeefster</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <span class="Latn" lang="en">commissioner</span>, one who commissions an action.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:omdat.html>Omdat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:grondstof.html>grondstof</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:meer.html>meer</a> leverbaar <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:moest.html>moest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:annette.html>Annette</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:opnieuw.html>opnieuw</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:onderhandelen.html>onderhandelen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:met.html>met</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:opdrachtgever.html>opdrachtgever</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:annette.html>Annette</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> to renegotiate with the <b>commissioner</b> because one resource wasn'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> available anymore.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">at</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:eens.html>eens</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">once</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:eisen.html>eisen</a></i>

***opgaan.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:opgaan.html>opgaan</a> (10219)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">opgaen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">upgān</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gaan.html>gaan</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:opgaan.html>opgaan</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to go up, ascend
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zon.html>zon</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gaat.html>gaat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></b> in <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:oosten.html>oosten</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gaat.html>gaat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:onder.html>onder</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:westen.html>westen</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>The sun <b>goes up</b> in the east, and goes down in the west.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>to be a candidate, to make an attempt, to make a <a href = vnd.unilang:bid.html>bid</a> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">for a test, prize etc.</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>, to be tested
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ga.html>ga</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:morgen.html>morgen</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mijn.html>mijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:examen.html>examen</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>I'm <b>taking</b> my exam tomorrow.</dd></dl></dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:na.html>Na</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hun.html>hun</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:laatste.html>laatste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:overwinning.html>overwinning</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ging.html>ging</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> team <b><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:finale.html>finale</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>After their last victory, the team <b>made a <a href = vnd.unilang:bid.html>bid</a></b> for the <a href = vnd.unilang:finals.html>finals</a>.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>to hold true, to apply, to be significant
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>Die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:regel.html>regel</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geldt.html>geldt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:normaal.html>normaal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wel.html>wel</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gaat.html>gaat</a></b> in <a href = vnd.unilang:dit.html>dit</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geval.html>geval</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></b>.</i>
<dl><dd>That rule normally applies, but does not <b>apply</b> in this case.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li>to blend in, to be <a href = vnd.unilang:lost.html>lost</a> (in a crowd, surroundings etc.)
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:dankzij.html>Dankzij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> camouflage <b><a href = vnd.unilang:gaat.html>gaat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:luipaard.html>luipaard</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:helemaal.html>helemaal</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></b> in <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:omgeving.html>omgeving</a>.</i>
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:thanks.html>Thanks</a> to its camouflage, the leopard completely <b>blends in</b> with its surroundings.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be <a href = vnd.unilang:lost.html>lost</a> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">in an activity, so as to lose track of time, one's surroundings, etc.</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
